--- 帖子 #1 ---
5m Kevinator retracement system Majors only(eurusd*usd/chf*gbpusd*aud/usd*usd/cad)5 m chart only.

This system is a trend following system that uses the multi time frame stochastics as a definition of the current trend the market is in. If the market is stepping up then you take buy retracement bars.If the market is stepping down you take the sell retracement bars.

Retracement bars are the magneta(purple) bars on the indicator on the bottom.If the market is stepping down you take the downward magneta bars as entry.If the market is stepping up you take the upward magneta bars as entry.

LONGTERM

You can either enter the market (long term) when the mtf stochastics is changing directions and hold until trend is done or at any of the retracement bars going in the direction of the trend and hold (20-400pips)

SHORTTERM

You can scalp the market by finding the direction of the current trend (stepping up or stepping down) and entering the retracement bars and taking 5 to 20pips profit.

There are two ways to trade this system but the entry rules are solid.We have a solid method to define a trend (mtf stochastics) and a solid entry method ( enter on retracements).

It is up to you how much profit you take as you could be following a trend for days or just scalping all day long for short profits.

UPDATE /1/

*Retracement finder modified fix to display magneta on current bar (0) attached***********

UPDATE /2/

*Double woody CCI added to replace rf finder as well as autotrendline for more visual confirmation.

--- 帖子 #50 ---
Every trade you see in this thread are from sunday 5pm est until right now the trades which I am currently still in aud/cad/gbp.So if you can count for yourself and see how many that equals.

I trade when I am awake morning noon and night although if you are just beginning I would recommend london newyork session as it is fast paced.

TMA--If you have been trading long enough you will notice that almost every mt4 indicator will redraw itself in some way.

I know new traders brains just want to find that one indicator to use as a standalone.Unfortunately this does not exist so we use a combination of indicators in a "system" to get around this problem.

Redrawing would be a problem if we just used one indictor but since we use multiple indicators it is not a problem.

Also our trigger which is retracement finder does not redraw only the magneta does not refresh once loaded.I have been using it so long I dont even notice I just take the first bar up or down and keep it moving.

--- 帖子 #95 ---
Some of the best trades are taken when mtf stoch is trending in one direction and price pulls back to the opposite TMA then you take the next retracement bar in the direction of the trend.

If you trade in this way you will never lose one trade although you will have to wait for trade setups.If you scan many pairs you will have a more productive session.

Let me clarify what I just said...If mtf stoch is trending in one direction.....then Price in the TMA band will go in the opposite direction until it hits the band in the opposite direction of Mtf stoch........then you will take the next retracement bar in the direction of the mtf stoch..

It is like standing in front of a object with a ball in your hand...winding back and throwing the ball forward.

Pullback then major energy release...

--- 帖子 #99 ---
The retracement finder indicator has a refresh problem.Once it is loaded It will not show magneta on the current or future bars.There is a updated  version on the page before this one.

In the rule this was show to illustrate exactly how to trade the system and at which points to take positions.

Even if the indicator does not show magneta it really does not matter.

Very simple rules...Look at the mtf stoch for direction. Enter on the RF indicator bar in that direction.

So if mtf stoch say market is stepping up you will wait until rf finder indicator has bar up.Vice versa on the opposite trade.

Or you can take the pull back trade like in one of the pictures.That is the safest trade to take although you will have to wait for the setup.If you are impatient I suggest opening many charts and scanning them all.At the least you will begin to learn market movement.

Tradiing during the london and newyork session yields the best results.I trade all day so now 10,20,30 pips unless aussie news .Later 20 to 150pips moves.

You will have to learn to navigate the terrain and pick your spots.You will also have to learn to manage your money correctly.I am here to put you on more trade setups.

--- 帖子 #134 ---
P.Dean,

Get the money and go on to the next trade.

The type of trade that you hold is a pullback reversal.

1)you see how the mtf stoch is stepping up.

2)Price pulled back to oversold

3)price sling shot to the top

reverse conditions for short hold conditions

This is a momentum trade as trend is up and market pulled back to oversold but 60m mtf stoch says trend is still up.You take the next bull bar and hold.

Thats how you make most of your money for the day.

--- 帖子 #192 ---
Ok guys...

I thought I'd lend Kevin a hand and provide some basic training in PA and reading the indicators. So pull up a 5M GU chart and follow along.

You can see from the open of today (Friday) price sort of slowly made it's way higher but with no real momentum to speak of. We have a long period of consolidation (between re lines) and we see the stoch is over 80 but very flat. During the London session price makes a nice run up and creates a higher high but note that the stoch stays basicly flat even during what appears to be a nice run up. When I see a run up to a new high like that and the stoch doesn't respond that tells me that there's not alot of momentum behind the push higher. What I look for next is price to start making lower highs and the stoch to step down below the 80 level. As you can see on the first red arrow price comes down but doesn't quite make it tot he bottom of the TMA band but that's ok. Next I wait for a retrace to the upper band and see if price gives me another swing top that is lower than the last high. Low and behold we get the retrace to the upper band (second red arrow). Once we get the second retrace I start to get real interested and start to watch what price does around the upper band. Next you see a small pin bar form at the band high and the next candle is a nice bearish push down. Notice where the stoch indicator line is, it just stepped down below the 80 level. At the close of the bearish candle I would enter (green line) at 1.6427. My SL would go above the last swing high which is the first red arrow. Price makes it's way down to the bottom TMA band for a 14-16 pip gain. On the retrace indicator I like to see the bars come up on the positive side and then go below the zero line. The bar on the retrace indy doesn't necessarily have to turn magenta/red for me to enter the trade. I just like to see the indy bar go below as the bearish candle closes.  Now we wait to see if we get another retrace and price makes it's way back up to the upper band. Now we wait and watch what price does. Again, the stoch is still stepping down and price gives us a nice bearish candle as the retrace indy bars go below zero (3rd red arrow). I would be in at 1.6417 (green line). Also note we have another lower high formed.

I hope this doesn't confuse anyone. If you're patient and wait for the retraces you can put the odds in your favour.

--- 帖子 #194 ---
Hi Guys...

Just one more chart showing what's happened to the GU after the big 80 pip move down.

After the big move down price starts to go up and then back down this goes on for some time and you realise that we are in some type of consolidation pattern again (red lines). Take a look at the stoch during the consoildation. It's below the 20 level and basicly flat. Now you could take a long trade when the consolidation breaks but I would want to see some confirmation before I go long. Looking at this chart conformation would be for price to go above the aqua horizontal line at the last major swing high. Take a look at the swing A-B all the price action in the consolidation phase is inside of that last swing. For price to go significantly higher it has to break the swing high at 1.6438. Even if we break the consolidation area to the up side if price doesn't make it past 1.6438 and it turns around and starts lower price will have form another lower high within the A-B swing (see the aqua zig zag lines).

Maybe I am complicating things for some of you, but if you start to learn this stuff you will put the odds on your side and your winning percentage will go up significantly.

--- 帖子 #218 ---
Take a look at this 5 M GU chart. See how the stoch has been under 20 and relatively flat for hours. Notice price, we have been in a narrow range. When you see this combination it's a NO TRADE ZONE. Also note the TMA bands are getting closer together. This just means when we break out of the consolidation phase we should get a good move. Word of caution, there are times when the first move out of these zones is a false move. These happen alot just before or right at the London open. I am not saying this is always the fact but be aware of it. This is why I use PA to help me read the move. To go higher I need to see higher highs and higher lows, to go lower I need to see lower highs and lower lows.

--- 帖子 #221 ---
Here is an advanced technique. I would suggest if you are a newbie to learn the basic trading entry before attempting this trade. For those people who understand divergence here is an advanced trade entry that will just give you more confidence and confirm your entry.

On the 5M chart add the MTF Stoch and set it to 5 minutes so it reflects the candle formation on the 5 M chart. Now take a look at my picture. We have a long up trend and price starts to weaken and and lose momentum. When you see this start to look at the 5M stoch. As you can see we have higher highs on price but lower highs on the 5M stoch. Once I see this I start to look for pullbacks that don't exceed the last high. Examine the chart closely and you'll see 3 entries. Entry 1 is the most aggressive. It's taken with a minor pullback to the top band and price does not go higher then the last high. Entry 2 is after we had a touch of the bottom band and a pullback to the top band. When price reaches the top band I start to look for PA and the entry short. After entry 2 price goes to the bottom band and again pulls back to the top band. I follow the same process each time. Observe price action when price gets to the top band. When I see a nice bearish candle we have entry #3 which is the most conservative. Price is making lower highs as we move down. Notice the retracement indicator on each of the pullbacks...what is it doing??? Notice the 60 min Stoch, see how it is stepping down as we take these trades.

This is a picture perfect counter trend trade that turns into a full reversal that goes for the entire day on the 5 M chart.

--- 帖子 #251 ---
I feel you would benefit by using the Color Stochastic that Kevinator provided in Post #204. This clearly shows whether you are looking for a step up (long trade) or a step down (sell trade).. Don’t forget to make the adjustments to the indicator as stated in the post.

Just because the next magenta color bar of the Retracement Finder is showing above the 00 line in the chart you posted does not mean you forget the stochastic is showing you a short trade.. Have a look to see what would have happened had you waited for the magenta color bar to be below the 00 line…………it would have been a winning trade.

You need to be patient and look at what the chart is telling you and check that you have obeyed the rules before trading.

Go back over the rules that Kevinator provided in the Word document and using the rules, go over the charts applying them If you do that, I’m sure you will get a better result.

I hope this helps.

--- 帖子 #270 ---
As I put in the post above your last one, until the hour closes the stoch will change colour and until the 5min candle closes it will change colour.  Until you get the hang of it, try taking trades when the stoch (closed stoch) is going one way and the price gets to the outer reaches of the bands (or as close as possible) and then take the trade in the direction of the stoch.  It takes practise and thats what demo is for.

--- 帖子 #285 ---
This is a MOM trade.

Mtf stoch is stepping down or up (down in this case).

Notice within the TMA band price is going in the direction of the mtf stoch.

Price then pulls back to the top of TMA band (Pullback)...but...mtf stoch still says market stepping down.

After price hits the top of the TMA when market is stepping down the result is a release of market energy with enough MOMentum to take price through the bottom or top of opposite band in the direction of mtf stoch.

This is the best trade setup of the system.Although you will have to wait for this setup to occur and only happens a few times a day.This type of trade will yield the most profit of 20 to 150 pips.

In this type of trade you catch those huge news bars of 70pips,90pips when the energy is released.

--- 帖子 #288 ---
My friend..

if you try to fix the repaint of the 1hr stoach, you will not get the early entry, which is the corner stone of this system...

if you replace the 1hr stoach.. i will assure, you will end up with -200 a day instead of +200 a day..  1hr stoach filters a lot of premature signals.. just enough and if one tries to flirt with it and filter more,  than it means missing a lot of good early opportunities or entry in the later stage of the swing/run which would damage the hit ratio..

I recommend to go with whats been laid out already... get in for more valid trades relentlecly and manage your trade after trigger.. if it runs in your direction try to keep it and bank at first real threat against your position and quickly move on to the next trade.. it could be +10 +20 +25 maybe sometimes +40 + ... scan scan scan..

keep it simple..  you hear the alert sound.. check the chart.. than check the 1hr stoach... if its stepping in the direction of the signal.. bammmmmmm set the order and go for it.

I hope it helps.

ps) Kevin if i am out of line let me know brother..

--- 帖子 #318 ---
not easier than this.

Set UseStochFilter to true and only alarm will ring if RF is inline with stoch, but..

If you set StochShift to 0(zero) it compares the actuall Stochvalue with the last closed stochvalue

if you set StochShift to 1 it compares the last closed Stochvalue with the Stochvalue one hour before (hope you understand)

cheers

Mediator

--- 帖子 #328 ---
Hi

The BigMo is a moving average EMA89

I use a MA in color, so if price is above BigMo is black I prefer long signal and vs for short.

The entry indicator is a indicator I look at for help me timing my entrys.

If I say look for a short trade and RF give signal Stoch look right I then look at entry timing if it is yellow or Red and coming from top going down I take the trade.

If I get a long signal and BigMo is still bearish(white) I take the long trade if I have around 20-30 pips to BigMo. Because many times you will se price hit the BigMo and stall reverse or smash threw. But atleast it give me a signal to have finger on bail button if I am in a trade

And entry timing also help me to see if I have divergense.

I attach a chart, hope it helps you

--- 帖子 #427 ---
This system can be easily backtested correctly taking into account the repainting of the TMA indi and the "repaint" of the MTF stochs (which isnt really a repaint, the same thing will happen with all MTF indi's)

Simply use one of the many trading simulator EA's that are available, this will allow you to blast through a daily 5m chart in about 45mins and see the changes as they would occur in real time.

I personally use the LFH Trading simulator (which is available freely on this forum)

Simply looking at the charts of past times is not really backtesting anyway, the only way to truly backtest is to either forward test, or run the historical data forwards again (which is what most trading simulators do).

Regards, John

Hello

Attached here and in the 1st post is a updated version of the system.

Retracement finder is a modified version of double woody CCI.I have added this indicator as a replacement although they are one in the same.

Auto trendline is the other addition to the system.This indicator will allow you to visually understand exactly were you stand within the trend.

When price begins to break the trend line that is a early warning that the current trend is over and price is changing directions like in the photo.

This should keep you out of trouble when looking to determine direction of trend.

This also adds another potential play to the system which is the buying and selling of the trendline break as well as the hard rules of the system.

--- 帖子 #466 ---
Those are MOM trades.

If you are just selling and buying at the top and bottom of the TMA that will work for a while as the market is ranging nicely.

When the market starts trending hard the highs will get higher and higher and higher without the retracement to the bottom tma.

Hindsight it is hard to describe this situation even with a screen shot.It is something you will have to experience.

So If you are to trade that way be ready to exit when the market is overbought or oversold on the tma but continues to make higher highs or lower lows.

Variations are fine but you must leave the bare bones of the system as it is no additional indicators added and find a way to work with what is laid out already.

If additional indicators are added and they do not pan out this will only lead to confusion.

--- 帖子 #470 ---
Hello

Yes I would have taken the long position.According to your indicators the 4hr and 60M mtf stoch are in agreement.

In this case I would let price action run its course and push higher highs.If you are trading in consolidation for some time then there is a breakout making higher highs it is our first instinct to try to pick a high for reversal.

You should follow the trend and react to what the market is actually doing at the moment.If you have the 4hr and 60 in agreement you will usually get a strong push to the top or bottom.

There will always be a pull back after a strong surge to the top.

I noticed that shortly after that there was a change in trend on the 60m chart.Then Price fell below the upper tma then returned.

This was a really good MOM trade which is the highest probability setup we have and can be traded with max lots.

After that 60m and 4hr returned to agreement and long trend resumed so keep pushing higher and higher.

Economics drives these events so do not think in terms of I am looking for a reversal when 60m and 4hr are in agreement.Follow the money trail as far as it will take you.

Always in the back of your mind keep the MOM trade formation fresh and learn it like you know how to get to your local grocery store and can spot the route day or night.

--- 帖子 #490 ---
No..It is not as simple as just buying over sold tma and selling overbought tma.

If you scroll back in your charts a few days you will notice instances were there are huge drops that keep going and going for 100+ points.

You do not want to get caught in that spot because the market drops fast and without warning.

It is like the market is teasing you with those kind of situations and the first time you drop your disciplined approach the very next bar will drop double what it just gained.

Have you ever noticed a market creeping up slowly for hours, then in a matter of two bars it drops triple what it took four hours to build up to?

You do not want to get caught in that situation.If you follow the system you will have turned down those trades like the one in your screen shot but....will have gained the large bars that destroyed what took hours to build.

So stay sharp and do not fall for everything that they throw at you.

Take the bait and get burned.You see how if you had bought at the oversold tma market would have reversed on you?

--- 帖子 #620 ---
No worry Peter

System is evolving...60M stoch is for regular short trades which can be confirmed with 240.

If you are taking the 60 and the 240 does not match then be aware that the overall trend(240) is not going in the direction of the 60 so get in and get out.

If 60 and 240 match you can expect a bigger move for more profit.

MOM or "slingshot" trades are taken from the 240 in the direction of the overall trend.

I enter on the first rf bar and not after the close.That way I get a better price.

--- 帖子 #666 ---
Look at the 240 stoch...it is red.So wait until price hits the upper band of the TMA.Then sell if.....240 stoch is still red.

So as of now price is trending down.Wait until price pulls back to the top of the TMA.At that time if the 240 stoch is still red then the down trend is still valid and price will continue down.

Your entry point is at the top of the TMA band.

So 240 stoch is red and wait for the pull back to the top of the tma and sell.

Use the RF to enter downward.

The Divine ( Post 651 )

I don't know if you have cured your problem with your MT4 but I had a similar problem a few months ago where my MT4 of long standing kept freezing my computer.

After much trial and error I realised that it was an update to my anti-virus (or maybe it was my firewall) that caused the problem, so I removed my MT4, closed my firewall and anti-virus whilst I re-loaded my MT4. Once loaded I re-opened my antivius and firewall.

I haven't had a problem since.

--- 帖子 #742 ---
For those who has similar problem, here is the solution:

- close your MT4

- go to MT4 indicators folder (C:/MT4/experts/indicators/)

- delete all EX4 files which have MQ4 files

- DON'T DELETE EX4 files which not have MQ4 files

- start your MT4

For the example, you have 2 files :

- Color Stochastic v1[1].04.ex4

- Color Stochastic v1[1].04.mq4

Delete only  Color Stochastic v1[1].04.ex4

But if you have only EX4 without MQ4 file, DON'T DELETE it.

MT4 crashing problem usually because the EX4 files previously created by a newer version MT4 than your have right now.

Deleting all EX4 will force your MT4 to create a new EX4 (which has same version with your MT4) from MQ4 file.

Hope this will help all of you.

--- 帖子 #762 ---
Hi All

as I am trying to scan as many possible low spread pairs as possible (and often from my laptop so SMALL screen!!) I have re-written and improved the alerting capabilities.

In this version it is also easier to see the last step (up/down) for both stochs as this is displayed as text at the left of the indicator.

There are 2 indicators required:-

TMA Called - this just needs to be in your indicators folders - DO NOT add it to your chart

!Kevinator - this replaces the color stochastics indicators being used for 1 & 4 hr, both are in the same indicator

The defaults should be fine as specified by what Kevinator uses.

The only parameters you need to worry about are

a) if you use a different CCI period than 8

b) how stringent you want the MOM trades to be

By default a possible MOM trade will be alerted for long if:-

Both stochs are stepping up

CCI is now above 0 and was previously below 0

Current price is below the mid line

(reverse obviously for short)

If you wish to be less stringent with MOM trades (ie, for strong trending markets when price doesnt always retrace back to the opposite band)

you can set the parameter xb_MOM.Mid to false

then the price needs only to have retraced to the upper line for long trades, lower line for short trades

A possible long scalp trade will be alerted if:-

Hourly stoch is stepping up

CCI is now above 0 and was previously below 0

Current price is below the mid line

(reverse obviously for short)

Trade signals are based on the current bar to give the earliest possible  indication, just because a signal is given within a bar doesn't mean  that by the time the bar ends the signal is still valid.

NOTE:- an alert is a poor substitute for scanning the charts manually, but sometimes can be helpful

Regards

John

--- 帖子 #785 ---
We are all being brought up to speed as to what is going on.

Three strategies.

1st) 60M/Last week we focused on taking short trades for quick 10, or 20 pips.

To do this we used the 60m stoch only.We have been getting used to scanning charts for setups.Entering trades on the rf finder and exiting trades with profit.

2nd)240/ This week we are focusing on MOM or momentum trades.We are looking at the 4hr chart  and buying and selling according to the direction of the 4hr stoch.When price pulls back to the top of the TMA on a down 4hr stoch we sell and vice versa.

We are doing strictly 240 this week.

3rd)60m and 240m/ Next week we put it all together and Mix the methods.We will be taking every pip that is not tied down.

The MTF stoch does not repaint.

--- 帖子 #839 ---
There is no such thing as over bought/sold in trending markets with the stochastic.

During trending markets indicators such as the stochastic will stay within their over sold/bought zones for the majority of the trend, as these indicators readings are capped with how high and low they can go 0-100 they will stay within that zone during strong trends.

All of this over bought/sold stuff is novice talk, and it is one of the thing/problems that leads new and novice traders to fail.

Yes there is pullbacks within trends but if price is falling and it pullsback, it does not mean its over bought, vice-versa for longs, remb one thing the stochastic is an oscillator, it was built/created/mathamaticlly programmed for ranging bound markets, not for trends.

So basiclly you are using a screwdriver to hammer in a nail.

Hi All

again to make things easier for me as often I have to work from a small screen.....

because MT4 rescales the charts constantly sometimes the TMA bands can look close together when in actual fact there is quite a bit of distance in terms of pips between them.

without getting the crosshairs out - this can be hard to see, and has meant in the past I have not taken some trades because on initial glance the distance to the next band didn't seem worth it (we are talking mainly the short term scalps not the MOM trades).

I have made a slight modification to the TMA indicator to display the distances in Pips between the Bid price and the bands.

NOTE:  NO MODIFICATION HAS BEEN MADE TO THE LOGIC OF TMA

--- 帖子 #869 ---
Hi All

just noticed a small display bug in the !Kevinator indicator (after looking at Kevinator's recently posted charts).

This bug only appears if you switch the Stoch timeframes in the parameters AFTER you have already had the indicator on your chart.

ie. load the indicator with the defaults, ie. 1hr, then change to 30m after the indicator has already displayed.

what happens is the little text which shows the Timeframe and Direction is left on and overwritten with the new timeframe

To get rid of the old timeframe object

press CTRL + B to get the objects list

search for the objects with the name "!2TFStoch.Desc.xxx" and "!2TFStoch.Dir.xxx" where xxx is the original timeframe you loaded the indicator with, and then delete them

As stated - this bug is a DISPLAY bug only, the logic is not affected in any way.

Regards, John

60M Mtf stoch and 240 mtf stoch

Last week we were learning how to use the 60m stoch and TMA in order to take short trades of 10and 20 or so pips profit.We made many trades this way with much success.

This week we are focusing on MOM or MOMentum trades which using the 240 stoch as a guide for trend direction and waiting for TMA to hit opposite TMA against the direction of 240 trend then the next rf signail in the direction of the 240 trend which will result in a energy release.20 to 200+ pips profits.Must use discipline and wait for trade setups.

Next week we will put it all together and mix the 60 and 240 techniques of week 1 an 2 for an all out tradeathon.Taking short and long term trades.

If you can negotiate these obsticles successfully this will be a moment of enlightenment.

--- 帖子 #894 ---
Hi Logic38,

This is my take on $/Yen at the moment (80.75 as I type)

1) 4H stoch are red (down): this is the most important (it favours shorts)

2) 1H stoch are green (up): if you are looking for a short term long trade then look for the price to be at the bottom of the TMA and then an UP Magenta bar for a quick 10/20 pips, possibly to the top of the TMA band.

But because of 1), I would be more inclined to look for a short setup

3) the short setup would need:

a) the price at or above the top of the TMA band

b) depending on whether you are a more conservative trader or not, you could wait for

1) a down Magenta bar

2) 1H stoch goes red (down)

or simply take the short at the TMA band. In both cases, initial Target Point would be near the bottom of the TMA at 80.57

I welcome any comment if I have got anything wrong

Kevin if you will allow me a moment.  None of this is trying to be negative just concerns/questions about the system and how things are done.

I stumbled upon this thread by accident, I actually clicked on the wrong link while it was on the first page.  I've been looking at it cause something about this had me interested.

First love the mom trades.

1.  Yes, in a trending environment a stoch can and will stay in an overbought or oversold level for a VERY long time.  If you actually see the 5 min stoch much of the time when it hits the far bands, the 5 min info is showing the opposite of the OB or OS of the 4 hr.  So basically we are buying/selling on a pull back once price action starts to go back in the direction of the original trend.  If you look at a higher TF charts you would not even see that blip on the screen.

2.  The other thing I like about this are the indicators, and this is coming from a guy that normally trades naked.  Loving the MTF stoch.

3.  It can get the new folks looking at some price action and let them see the where and hows price is moving and that will help them incredibly over the trading career.

Kevin, I do have some concerns/questions for you I would like to ask about.

1.  yesterday I asked about trading into news and never got a response.  Over time it is a common belief, mine also, that is very dangerous.  I understand if you have a longer term trade on you may keep it on depending how far into profit you are.  how do you handle news?

Again, this is something that would have people concerned about the trades as I can say I personally will filter those trades out as not a high percentage trade.  Once again, that is me personally and how I trade.

I understand this has a lot to do with the trader's own personality and trading style but it must be something they understand.  You've had a few traders in here totally confused about when they should get out and why.  These are valid questions you have point blank refused to answer.  Understanding why, where, and how to get out of trade can be even more important than how to get into it.

4.  From looking at the system, and from what i know about trading, this system could (maybe should?) trade different depending on weather the pair/market are trending or not.  What is your take on this?

I think answering some of these questions would really help a lot of people and also stop some of the people that come on the this thread and act as a distraction.

News trading is the single key driver of the market.Without it there would be no market movement at all.There is always someone speculating or reacting to some news event.

Interest rate decisions are the number one news event in the market today.Governments move large pools of money to the country that can provide the best rate of return and the FOMC minutes anouncement is the best event to follow.Non farm and employment are mid level drivers.

We do not concern ourselves with these anouncements because we are not spike traders.In fact we encourage those large spikes here because they are either the push to put us at the top or part of the pull back to TMA entry.

Money management is your concern.I am not a accountant and do not know your balance,broker or personal financial goals.My role is to put you on  better trade setups faster.You determine your risk and reward.

As long as all the signals match and are valid we will take positiions.We look to the 240 for confirmation which is the major trend.

I can deal with any and all situations that arise on this forum.I am aware that 97% of traders on this forum are good and genuinely want to learn.I am also aware that there are alot of traders with thousands of posts who still have a day job and have failed to learn anything of use and are interested in their own prestige and not in the assistance of other traders success.

The other 3% are like computer viruses.They cruise from thread to thread with the same concerns?Does it repaint?What kind of money do you make?Why this and why that? Every indicator of any use in metatrader repaints for the simple reason that they report things as they are now.

They are the type that has not realized that fact and are still trying to find that one stand alone indicator.It does not exist...to get around this problem we use a combination of indicators in a "system".

I am not offended by your questions as I can tell that they are real concerns and not the one sided questions of a angry person stating an angry point in the form or a question....do you understand what I am saying by that statement?

I wish success to the community and more profit to everyone.

--- 帖子 #921 ---
Hi Pete,

If both were green then technically there was nothing wrong with taking a Long near the bottom of the TMA once you get an UP magenta bar for a quick 10/20 pips to the top of the TMA.

I will say this though: around the time of both entries the 4H stoch, although slightly green, was still very low (9.3514 on my chart) and we were quite clearly still in a downtrend; as you know the market can carry on staying oversold for a long time but still make make new lows (effectively that trade could be seen as trying to 'pick a bottom' and these trades are notoriously dangerous - on these occasions, I would try to put my stop at b/e asap).

Also, but i can't confirm, i believe that the #MT-Trendline was pointing down too at the time.

With these 2 factors in mind, it might have been more prudent to wait for the market to hit the top of the TMA bands and take a short trade once the MOM criteria are all aligned (see posts 892/896/897 for a similar setup on usd/jpy earlier on today).

I know that it's easier to say all this with hindsight as GBP ended up going further down, but with a pair like Cable that can move a lot and fast, these 'pick a bottom trade' need fast fingers and good money management for your s/l place. I would be more confident in scoring 'pick a bottom' pips on a slower moving pair

--- 帖子 #936 ---
I think you're a bit hard on yourself here: Kevin & I agreed from our respective posts that apart from the downtrend, you ticked all other 4 boxes for a long trade based on the 1H stoch/RF strategy:

1) 4H stoch green (a bonus)

2) 1H stoch green

3) price having gone below the TMA and rising above it

4) you had your magenta bar

Also bear in mind that every trend that changes will likely start with the 1H stoch changing first.

There were a few other possible Long Sterling trades based on the 1H strategy (2) 3) & 4)) since then (all London times); these are based on how the stoch looks now (it might have been different then but at least you can see what i mean):

.09.05: i would not take it, too close to top TMA

.11.35: 19 possible pips & 9 pips drawdown

.13.45: 29 possible pips & 5 pips drawdown

.14.35: i would not take it, too close to top of TMA

.15.10: 14/32 possible pips & 15 pips drawdown

.15.35: i would not take it, too close to top of TMA

So you see, there are pips to be made even counter-trending and on most occasions a 16 pips (+ spread) stop loss would have been enough.

THIS IS ONLY MY VIEW AND ANYONE PLEASE FEEL FREE TO COMMENT/DISAGREE...:

I suggest that you (and anyone else that hasn't got years of trading behind them), pick just 1 pair and study it day after day to get a good feel for it with both 1H & 4H strategies; there is a normal tendency because there are so many pairs available to want to trade loads of them at the same time, but from my experience, it's better to be really good with one pair than average with many ("jack of all trades and master of none" type of thing). Once you're proficient with one pair, introduce another and so on. I appreciate that there are many that can instantly grasp a strategy and apply it to any instrument, but this is for the others like me who aren't little Einsteins lol

Keep a written journal where for each signal you keep a track of things like: time of signal, drawdown, most pips achievable, after how many pips could you have put your stop at b/e ... and anything else that you feel is relevant to YOUR way of trading (it's a known fact that give 10 traders the same exact strategy and you will get 10 different amounts of pips achieved). Get to 'know' your chosen pair, get a feel of how it moves and behaves.

Most important: you will not be wasting any time doing this even if you only paper trade:

1) the market and all pairs will still be there tomorrow

2) Kevin's strategies are such that you will rarely have to wait a long time to get a new signal.

Last but not least, a big thank you to Kevin for sharing this with us.

--- 帖子 #964 ---
Hi Adji,

not quite, the system is based on 2 types of entry

MOM trades, this is based of the 4hr stoch, and is when the stoch is one way (eg down) and the price has retraced to the upper band, in such a case you take the first valid RF bar for short.

In such cases the hourly doesnt really matter as it is probably going the opposite way anyway because of the retracement, however at some point the hourly stoch should come back into line with your 4hr stoch.

the other entry is the short term trades (ie. band to band), in these trades the hourly stoch is important.

ideally for these trades you are looking to trade in the direction of the hourly stoch on the first RF bar from the opposite band - the closer you are to the target band the riskier the trade.

so example, Hourly stoch is long, you would be looking to enter a buy trade on the first RF bar for long that is close to the lower band, with an aim to take profit close to the upper band, which is why the closer you can enter to the lower band the safer your trade.

of course you could be in a short term trade (band to band) and then the 4hr stoch comes into line, in which case your short term trade has turned into a MOM trade (this is what happened with my USDCHF trade from earlier)

Hopefully this answers your question.

Regards, John

I have been evaluating your system, Kevinator.  For most part it is profitable.  The entry setup is good.  However, it would still require  money management. If that person doesn't have a plan on what to do if the market goes against him, he will always be the recipient of losses.   Your system + money management= profitable trades.

--- 帖子 #1025 ---
Broker Times:-

I do not know why but I see a similar discussion in almost every thread I read nowadays regarding broker times & the differences.

In a system such as this which is not premised on placing an order at an exact time, but rather based on a combination of various technical indicators, broker time makes absolutely NO difference.

The system here is based on various technical indicators coming together to give a possible trade, it really doesn't care if your broker time is GMT, EST or the time on the moon (not really sure what timezone they have!).

The only differences will be that someone may get a signal that you don't get because of the broker time, that's OK, other times you will get signals they don't get.

In the end you can ONLY trade the signals provided by YOUR broker.

Incidentally, it is important to note, that even if you are on the same broker time as someone else but with a different broker, the signals will also be slightly different, as all feeds are broker based, not centralized.

I have two different brokerage accounts, both on GMT, one uses MT4 and the other JForex, even a simple thing like MA has slight differences.

Regards

John

--- 帖子 #1029 ---
Hi Takethat

Welcome to the wonderful world of Forex, until an organization such as the World Bank (I.B.S.) takes over control of the Forex market, this will always be the problem.

If you really want to have the same signals as the thread owner, then use his broker.

However as this is a thread and other people are posting from their own broker, someone might post a trade that you don't receive as a signal - does that mean their trade is invalid?

In addition, this (and other) forums has lots of different systems on it, posted by lots of different users, with different brokers - are you really going to open an account with every broker just to get the same signals as the thread owner?

As I stated at the beginning, these quirks exist due to the de-centralized nature of the market and will continue to do so, and there are only 3 solutions

a) accept it as part of the wonders of trading forex

b) open an account with every broker of the thread owner for the systems you use

c) switch to a more centralized method of investment (ie. stocks)

Regards

John

--- 帖子 #1063 ---
No problem new trader........you are the reason we are here and not for our

self glorification but so you can learn to survive.

240= 4hr stoch we look at that for overall trend direction.

Within the TMA band price will be trending in that direction.

For example purposes.We will say the 240 stoch is down,short,or selling.

Price within the TMA band is going down obviiously.

Price will pullback to the top of TMA when price is going down.

Then energy release in the direction of the trend.

The is called a MOM trade or MOMentum trade.

You must manage your own money as I do not know your broker,stop out level,margin requirements,leverage,or account balance.

I use a excel calculator to calculate these things so you must manage your own account.I am here to put you on more trade setups.

I am not sure if i agree with this (such) signals although according to the rules of the system it is a valid one.. but some commonsense will do good here in such situations..

price is clearly bullish.. TM band is striking bullish.. 240 stoach stepping up like crazy..  when such upward move is obvious even to a 5 year old by just looking at the chart... it is not wise to take a short scalp trade just because 1hr stoch flashed stepped down in the first 5-10 minutes of the hour.. and RF signaling down..

at some point a trader must use some commonsense to evaluate the whole picture and reject and wait for better opportunities..

The reason i have froze this pic is to help out the new traders as i see lots of them in this thread.. the reverse side of this could get nasty when PA makes a quick turn and runs up fast to hit the SL on the other side in a heart bit most times.. and this could ruin the confidence of a newbies of this system... a experienced trader might be able to get away with this for a small loss, but a experienced trader most likely will not get involved in such trade, I have no doubt.  its too risky because its simply going off on well premature PA reversal trade.

such trades must be taken on more of a slower days and not trending time of PA especially when it's still peaking..  more settled bands or days.. the trade on the first flash of the 1hr stoach is totally fine..   this must be recognized by a trader... and believe me you will not miss out on opportunities.. by god there are so many more right around the corner that you can take advantage of a bit wiser off more matured PA situation.

I only made this post out of care folks.. you can reject it or you can keep it in the back of your mind.. it's a free world brothers.

--- 帖子 #1109 ---
Hi Android38

the trade is perfectly valid by the rules.

P.Dean was mentioning that although the trade is valid by the rules, sometimes there are times when it is best not to take these scalp trades.

For me personally I look at the angle of the TMA bands, if they are not too much of an angle then I take the trade, if the angle is clearly bullish and a bearish scalp is indicated then i don't bother with it, but that is my own interpretation

having said that I probably miss quite a few good setups, but there are plenty of trading opportunities every day for me not to worry about missing a few.

Regards, John

--- 帖子 #1110 ---
that is not the version, you need to provide the build id

for example "Version 4.00 Build 402"

in some cases indicators that were originally compiled on a later build will not work on a previous build, in such cases you should

delete the indicator with the .EX4 suffix ONLY if you have the indicator with the .MQ4 suffix, Metatrader will then automatically rebuild it for you

For the one hour stochastics, click on the paperlip, select hide images, then download the !Kevinator or !Kevinator v1 indicator (either the MQ4 or the EX4)

Regards

John

--- 帖子 #1134 ---
Tal1983

If you have downloaded the Color Stochastic, you can change the "timeFrame" under the Inputs tab to 60. This will give you the 1 hour stochastic.

You can download the indicator again into the same window and have the "timeFrame" set to 240 for the 4 hour stochastic.

Make sure the you remove the tick for Fixed minimum and Fixed maximum on the Common tab of the indicator.

I'm not able to explain how you only show the 4 hour stochastic if you downloaded the !Kevinator v1 indicator as that automatically loads with both stochastics.

Di

--- 帖子 #1135 ---

--- 帖子 #1136 ---
Tal1983

They are both there in the same window. The 60 min one is the yellow/red/blue one and is the thicker of the two.

The 4 hour one is immediately underneath and you can see the Sea Green colour and the blue step riser. It is set to a 2 thickness whereas the other is set to a thickness of 4.

I admit to changing the color and thickness of my 4 hour stochastic.

Di

--- 帖子 #1139 ---
I can see both stochs quite clearly in your chart,

the one that is yellow with flashes of blue & red is the 1hr (the upper line)

the one that is sea green with flashes of blue & red is the 4 hr (the lower line)

you can also hover your mouse over the lines and it will show you what each line is.

In addition the bottom stoch window you have for 4hr is not needed when using the !kevinator indicators.

As someone also mentioned you are missing the TMA indicator on your chart (either TMA.ex4 or TMA with Distance.ex4)

--- 帖子 #1141 ---
Hi Dehyah

that was a valid signal

BUT

price had been clearly in a downtrend

4hr stoch had only changed to long within the 4hr period

The name of this thread is Kevinator 5m retracement

the operative word being retracement

while sometimes you may be lucky and catch the start of a new trend, more often you wont

P.Dean and myself have mentioned this, just because there is a valid signal doesn't mean you should necessarily take it

Kevinator has mentioned this is like a "football play book", you need to have studied the reactions in real time and in time you will be able to automatically discard the weaker signals

Don't worry this is a learning curve, but very quickly overcome, in the beginning I also was taking signals left right & centre, now I am more selective.

Keep on with it though, this is a two part process

1) recognizing the signals

2) recognizing the stronger/weaker signals

Regards, John

--- 帖子 #1148 ---
For those that are having a hard time visualizing what exactly we are doing with the MOM trades,

We are taking the large parts of the major trend.

If you see I have marked the 4hr chart to show the major trend.

This is the major trend your 240 or 4hr mtf stoch will show.

If you see the market surges up then,  pulls back , then resumes.

We are taking that surge in the trend and when price pulls back it pulls back to the top or bottom of the TMA.

Does this make sense to everyone and do you understand what we are doing?

--- 帖子 #1163 ---
In my experience opening chat rooms trends to be counter productive. No matter how well the methodology is defined everyone wants to use their own modifications and this leads to mass confusion, especially with the newbies. After about 3-4 weeks of in fighting amongst the group most people will lose interest, move on and the chat room dies. I've been trading for a long time now and I've been involved in a few chat rooms and this happens in almost every room I've got involved with. Even if you have a strong leader like Kevin, he can't be in the room 24/7 to keep people on track. Even if he could I would imagine he wouldn't want to be in the room 24/7 otherwise his trading account would suffer.

Again, just my two cents worth.

Hello Art

MOM=MOMentum

We first look at the 240 stoch for trend direction.

In this case the trend is up (4hr trend).

Within the TMA band price is moving upward.

We wait until price pulls back to the bottom TMA band and enter Long.

Exit is at the top of TMA or if you get a large spike and the market looks like it is going to keep going hold it.You may have the lowest price of a big move!

Vice versa for a short.Do you understand this.

I would begin trade at 12am est and end trade at 4pm est trading all the majors except usdjpy including eurjpy.

--- 帖子 #1214 ---
Hi Fratelli

in the settings of the Kevinator indicator is a parameter

xi_TMA

you set this to be the same period as your TMA, default is 56, but if you change your TMA on screen you must change it here as well.

Note the same applies to the CCI, there is a parameter xi_CCI which should be at the same settings as your retracement finder.

Regards

John

--- 帖子 #1232 ---
Hello

Do not be confused.What we are doing here is simple.

MOM=Momentum

We look to the 240 stoch which is the 4hr for overall trend direction.

We are trading the 5m chart with the majors minus usdjpy.We also trade eurjpy and sometimes gbpjpy.

If the 4hr stoch is going up we then look into the TMA channel.

Price should be going in the direction of the 4hr stoch.

When price pulls back to the lower channel we will enter a trade going in the direction of the 4hr trend.

So we are buying or selling pullbacks.Then a release of energy in the direction of the trend.

Exit is the top of the TMA...unless you get a good enough surge that you think price will continue then we will hold the trade and let it run.

If the 4hr stoch is in one direction we should get a good move.If the 4hr and the 1hr stoch match then we get a great move.

Primarily we are looking at the 4hr though.

Your first time trading use the retrace finder indi to enter in the direction of the 4hr stoch once it has bounced off the TMA.

If you have taken trades with us before just enter when price crosses the line as we know it will then continue in the direction of the major trend.

Surge in the direction of the major trend,..............pulll back (entry) to the opposite TMA............energy release in the direction of the major trend.

Surge in the direction of the major trend,..............pulll back (entry)to  the opposite TMA............energy release in the direction of the major  trend.

Surge in the direction of the major trend,..............pulll back (entry)to  the opposite TMA............energy release in the direction of the major  trend.

You are taking the major parts of the 4hr trend as it moves in its path.

We use the pullbacks as entry points.

New traders us the rf finder as a trigger to enter.

After you get a few trades you enter at the line.

Dear All

following different requests here are the latest versions of the indicators

IMPORTANT: The default parameters ONLY need to be changed if you wish to use some of the more advanced settings used by more experienced users of this system.  Otherwise the defaults are perfectly valid.

!Kevinator v2

Updates/Modifications

Ability to send eMails for alerts has been added (this does require that you have configured the parameters in MT4 to use this facility)

The control to send Alerts/eMails has been removed at the chart level.  This is now controlled at the Metatrader level.  ie. Alerts/eMails will either be sent for ALL charts that the indicator is attached to or none.

The default is no Alerts/eMails - to switch On/Off press F3 for Global variables.  Search for !Kevinator Alerts (or eMail) and set to 1 for On, 0 for Off.

Period seperators if required will now be displayed in the indicator window, (Default is to display, can be changed in the parameters), the first time frame (ie. the 1hr normally) has a vertical line of dots for the seperation, the second time frame (ie. the 4hr normally) has a solid vertical line for the seperation.

The color of the Text for Up/Down can now be modified.

The rules for MOM trade alerts has been corrected to ignore the step direction of the hourly stoch.

TMA with Distances

Updates/Modifcations

The color of the distances in pips can now be modified.

--- 帖子 #1247 ---
Hi Docrock

the numbers are simply there so you know the distances to the different bands, this is more important for the shorter term scalp trades.

Sometimes because MT4 rescales the charts the distances between the bands can visually look narrow, but in fact is quite a number of pips (especially after large moves up & down and you have a lot of candles on your chart)

The numbers are simply there to help you better gauge the risk involved, especially on band to band trades.

ie. The trade signal comes for long and the price is below the middle band so still valid, but the distance to the upper band (where you would normally be looking to exit for short term) is only 7 pips away, then it would be better to skip the trade - especially if for a correctly placed Stop at the swing is greater than this.

so simply put - the numbers are there to help you determine risk/reward

Regards

John

Hi

To use the eMail facility you need to find out the SMTP server of your eMail system

if you are using a "free" acct. such as Hotmail this information can be found on the web using google

SMTP server for hotmail is "smtp.live.com:25"

In MT4 press CTRL & O to get the options window

Switch to the eMail tabs

Set the check box "Enable"

Set the server to be the SMTP server

Set the logon to be your user id (in the case of hotmail your eMail address)

Password is your password

From & To should be your eMail address again

Press Test and check the journal to ensure you have everything setup

Regards

John

--- 帖子 #1254 ---
Hi

first of all exit MT4 and restart

MT4 has a bug where when you change some information in this eMail TAB it messes up the data, and can only be fixed by exiting MT4 and re-entering

then try Test again, if it still does not work, then exit MT4 and re-enter and change the 25 to 587

This usually occurs because your internet service provider has blocked port 25 for general access and the MT4 eMail system is very simplified.

If it still doesnt work after that then maybe it is something to do with the combination of MT4 build and your ISP and I cant help you.

For me with Hotmail it works fine.

Regards

John

--- 帖子 #1273 ---
Alerts on current simply means it will check values for the current open bar, otherwise it will check the last closed bar.

However if you use the Kevinator indicator then you don't need to have the alerts on the TMA, as these are already incorporated.

Regards

John

Cicak

the numbers at the end is the distance in pips from the current bid price to the line

I also noticed you have a couple of indicators twice on your chart.

You appear to have the TMA twice on your chart once only is enough (if you want the numbers to appear leave on the TMA with distances and remove the other TMA's)

You have the 4hr stochastic twice, once in the kevinator indicator (the sea green line) and once seperately

If that is intended (for instance because you want to try out different 4hr stoch settings) fine, otherwise the seperate 4hr stoch is not needed.

--- 帖子 #1415 ---
Reading some of the posts, it sounds like plenty of people are not 'experts' at using the MT4 platform; this post is for them.....

If you are like me, there will always be something on someone else's chart or template that you don't like:

.the colours of the TMA lines

.the colours of the candles or the background

.the width, colour & style of the Stochastic (some like 2 Stochs in 1 window, some like 2 separates windows)

.same with the Retracement Finder

.etc etc ...

Once you have 'designed' your chart with ALL the indicators needed for Kevin's system and it looks exactly the way you want it, do the following:

1) Click on 'Charts' near the top left (next to File, View, Insert)

2) Put your mouse above 'Templates' (8th line down): this will open a sub-menu

3) Click on 'Save Template'

4) Give that template a 'NAME' that you will easily remember

5) Click on 'Save'

Now open any other chart that you want to trade/study and set it to the 5 minutes timeframe:

1) Click on 'Charts' near the top left (next to File, View, Insert)

2) Put your mouse above 'Templates' (8th line down): this will open a sub-menu

3) Click on 'Load Template'

4) Find the 'NAME' that you've chosen in the previous step, Select it and click OK

This chart will now also be set EXACTLY how you like it and it is a lot quicker than having to amend someone else's template everytime.

Repeat the same with all the other pairs/instruments that you want to study.

If you are following more than one pair/instrument, personaly I find that it's a lot easier if they are ALL set the same and ALL set as I like it.

--- 帖子 #1447 ---
I have enjoyed myself today and made a lot of pips by: waiting for 1-Retracement to send a nice jingly alert checking that the H4 and H1 stochs are both heading in the same direction as the proposed trade checking that the market is within the TMA lines stop loss the most recent swing high/low take profit the opposite direction outermost TMA line adjusting the tp in line with TMA movement The attached makes mucking around with tp/sl a lot easier. It is an EA and lives in the Experts folder. Drag it onto the chart and it will draw a green tp and red sl line that represent the tp and sl of the open trade. If there are no stops already in place, it adds defaults.

After that, double click the green or red lines to highlight them. Moving them forces the ea to modify the trade's stops to reflect the new value of the moved line.

FYI, I have already coded a basic EA to trade this method. Before I release it, I want to trade manually and learn more about the strategy; whatever I learn I shall add to the EA. With any luck, you guys will be able to play with it by the end of the week. We shall see.

TMATrue doesn't repaint. The attached version doesn't have the pip distances, but it does accurately reflect where the channel was. There was great discussion of this in Nanningbob's trend trading thread, where it was explained that, in the present moment, both TMA indies are in the same place. It's only afterward that the 'pretty' one smooths itself out. For our purposes, I believe either one will work fine.

--- 帖子 #1469 ---
Hi Vickym

Kevin has mentioned this in a recent post:-

In effect - the retracement finder is there to help you in the beginning

as you get better in the logic behind the system the retracement finder becomes less necessary to the point that you are anticipating the retracement signal and entering before.

The retracement finder simply indicates that a retracement has taken place, in time, it is easier to see this purely from price action.

Regards

John

Everyone is entitled to their opinions. You can trust in EA's or not. They have advantages as well as disadvantages that users have to learn to live with.

I also think it's a good thing to keep the discusion of a trading system apart from the development of any EA related to it, and from what I've seen in SH's threads, that's his way of thinking too (He'll eventually open up a thread devoted entirely to his EA), so stop bashing this iniciative, there's room for us all, and also keep in mind that SH shares his work for free so what's with complaining ¿?

I do think that when using an EA it's important to be 100% familiarized with the strategy it's attempting to trade in order to spot bugs, errors and to prevent disaster. I don't beleive in "set and forget" EA's, at least not for real money

To end my post, I just want to say that any system that has a well defined set of rules is a good candidate for automation. We all know a bot doesn't have the "market feeling" some traders find necessary to trade, I personally find it's a really cheap price to pay in exchange for just watching money grow while jerking off to my favorite music or movies

Best wishes to all EA and non-EA traders

The TMA indicator is a "repainting" indicator, looking back at historical values is not possible (unless you use the "True" version)

However as this is about trading and not looking back at what might have been, the TMA is fine as is.

--- 帖子 #1487 ---
thinking about this what would be required

a) I am assuming you are talking about an MT4 dashboard, not a seperate application (which is possible but a lot more difficult)

b) what information would need to be displayed??

i) what quadrant the PA was currently in of the TMA, ie. OB/OS/Upper/Lower

ii) the current values up/down of the 4hr / 1hr stochs

iii) the retracement indicator value and it's direction increasing/decreasing

then of course the indi would need to have in it's parms all the pairs it is to monitor.

To create an indicator that did not need to have the other charts open would be possible but the processing required on each tick to calculate the data would mean you would have to have a very fast computer

the other option of course would be to have the existing Kevinator indicator (which currently monitors all this information anyway) post the values into memory, to be picked up by the dashboard which would run on it's own clean chart (ie. candles removed etc. so only dashboard is displayed)

All in all sounds like a very "doable" project.

--- 帖子 #1518 ---
P Dean offers good advice about getting on with it.

Trading is a business with associated costs. If you operate a business you are liable for a variety of costs such as rent, wages, insurances, phone etc, etc. You may well be into your 5th day or so  each week of running your business before you start seeing any real profit.

I don't know what it is with trading that a loss or two makes a lot of people run for the hills, or maybe on to another thread because this one "has failed". A losing day does NOT mean the system is a failure.

This is a great system and if you are a newbie it would be of great benefit to start at the beginning and read the whole thread, take notes, examine the charts attached to the threads to just get "involved" with the system.

Don't believe that trading is easy, it involves real work, real chart time, real patience and gratitude.

Thanks to Kevin for sharing his system.

Di

--- 帖子 #1553 ---
i had to step out for a hour..

guys... if you look at the major pairs they all are in a sideways move inside very a narrow band.. if you look at total movement they all are inside 50-60 pips range... so.. market is flat... this tells us it's time for scalp... so the OB/OS off the bands play key rolls..

once you get a alert.. quickly check on two things...

1) 1hr stoach position

2) PA 's band position..

if both are correlated with you signal than you got a valid signal.. take a shot..

at the moment there is no MOM setup until you get a movement outside the current band.. i can care or less what the 4hr stoach is saying now.. i got to see a movement now (swing) than pullback to the other side of band..

this is a momentum system.... what is the momentum now?... FLAT..

get involve on the scalp setup carefully and thoroughly when signal arrives.. than after trigger look for the reaction to the band.. see if brakes it firmly.. if it does maybe its worth the hold for a run.. if not and it's wish washy, bank the hell out of it and wait to see if it returns back to the run or it reverses inside the band again and maybe it will give you another scalp trade with a same chance for a run the other way..

this way you make your scalp trade to make little money and at the same time leave a slight door open to catch the run outside the box and then wait for MOM setup to take more profits..

sometimes if not at least the half time.. Market is not trending and it's either ranging or it takes direction which don't turn into a trend.. so that's why we use this combination.

i hope it helps or clears away.

regards,

Dean

--- 帖子 #1580 ---
This thread is becoming dangerously close to falling apart, I hope Kevin gets back soon to bring some order once again.

Yes there are repainting indicators involved, however the system works perfectly fine without repainting ones.

The TMA non-repainting version has been on the thread for quite a while, and if people search they can find non-repainting versions of the MTF stochastics, that don't flash in the trade direction, then opposite again.

The concept is sound, if you have problems with repainting and believing a system works, either forward test it, or replace the repainting ones with non-repaints.

I use both.  Picture below is with NON-repainting TMA and MTF Stochs, signals are still valid (notice to the left of the stochastics window, the indicator shows bullish & bearish movement within the same other time frame candle)

Regards

John

--- 帖子 #1607 ---
For everybody....

That's really a trader's discretion but at the same time you could add all these levels that could be in the area of the entry price:

.previous high/low

.fib level

.daily pivot/support/resistance level

.the list is endless

........

I'm a great believer of KISS (Keep It Simple Stupid) because the first thing that a lot of new(ish)-to-trading people will try to do is add this or that rule and make it more complicated than it needs to be although it's better to miss a trade because of an extra rule than enter a bad trade.

Here we have a fairly simple system provided by Kevin with straightforward(ish) rules so why not test the system using these said rules; that can be done live or paper trading, but if you use it AS IT IS at least you'll have an idea if it works, and if it works for you AND your personality (that's important too - not everybody has got the time nor the will to look at 5 minutes charts).

And if it works then and only then you can customise it to YOU: if you do it the other way round, more than likely you will end up trading a system that bears little relation to Kevin's original one.

Just my 2 cents/euro/pesos....

--- 帖子 #1621 ---
It's simply telling you that the Euro is at an important level where a few pips up or down makes the difference between:

.4H Stoch staying up (green) - still bullish although in o/b territory

.4H Stoch going red (down) - bearish

Dare I say in this situation you can get many contradicting signals during the 4H span as you will get many RF confirmations up AND down.

With an important vote in the Greek parliament today (re bailout), it might be wise to wait until that passes, because the market won't care whether the 4H (or any other indicator) is red or green when the result is announced.

--- 帖子 #1622 ---
Thanks ollieforex,  That's right.  The 4 hr has not completed yet, so it will still change color until the 4 hr is finished.

--- 帖子 #1674 ---
I don't know how much of the thread you have read.

There are 2 different systems in this thread, one for scalping using,among other things, the 1hr stochastic and the other being momentum trading using the 4 hr stoch.

There are Rules for the system attached to the first post in the thread. Furthermore, if you go to page 83 Post # 1235 you will see Kevin's run down on the momentum trading.

There are numerous examples throughout the thread on both systems.

One of the things I don't think you recognise as yet is that people may have their 4 hour time period starting at different times to other thread contributors because of the different brokers chart feed times. This can give opposing stochastic signals compared to some, so you have to decide which charts you want to use. There are oodles of brokers out there from where you can get demo MT4 charts. I use Go Markets (Aust), Alpari and Interbank. There first two have the same 4 hour period, the last starts the 4 hour period 2 hours later. So you have to find what you can live with.

John (jmw1970) recently posted a chart for a scalp trade. His Ultra Stochastic Color 30 min indicator is something with which I am not familiar, so I have no idea why he is using that instead of the Kevinator indicator. He is however, a generous contributor to this thread and may enlighten us as to his reasoning.

I hope this helps.

Di

--- 帖子 #1695 ---
you've hit the nail on the head...

1hr up - try to scalp to opposite TMA

4hr up - looking for past the TMA

1 & 4hr up - hoping for a big move

however regardless for me, my initial target is always the opposite TMA band, I make in-trade decisions at the mid-band and the target band

because sometimes what initially starts out as a scalp to the opp. band (ie. 4hr not in alignment) can change into a full blown high momentum trade.

In earlier posts when i post the entry, i generally also mention my thinking of what i am going to do (post 1672 is an example) this is not necessary to post BUT with all trades you should at least have in your own mind a plan of action.

John

you guys noticed my e/j exit..

i will explain you might find it useful..

two things were done on that trade which only and only relates to traders ability and skill which comes with experience, mental control and it is vital to one's success in market trading..

1) I did not quickly fold or panic when trade went against me so rapidly.. I let it settle out of the quick burst and sure risked getting the sl hit..(but since its within my range of my comfort risk, its ok)

2) did not get greedy and closed it for minimal loss once PA presented the opportunity.

not hoping or gettinggreedy to say, ok, now it will burst up to the upper band, let's wait to make profit out of it... now why? bcz i know my trading style.. our trading style is base on momentum release.. if don't pan out to that its time to look for the best way to get out for lesser loss..

PA and chart most times talks to us..

however there is a thin line between not making a panicy, premature exit and not waiting too long to exit.. and it comes with experience and many many trades executions under one's belt..

this is called my friends... being in control of situation and not the other way.

we got no set MM here... but this kinds of Live trades could show you different looks and forms in order to help you make your arsenal of trading better, i hope.

Hey Guys,

In response to some questions from earlier, I would like

to throw in my 2 cents. There are many ways to trade this

and I urge you to put the time in as this is a golden method.

Personally I will not be taking trades from the 60 minute (or less)

stochastic, only in the direction of the 4 hour (if it looks "right")

which I will explain here: in the first picture you see that the Euro

is saying 4hour is Up but when you look at the 4 hour chart with

the 10,3,3 linear weighted stochastic, it hasn't had a bullish

cross yet and it's a very strong down trend for the last 4 bars.

This doesn't look "right" to me and I will ignore the long trade.

So far during the last few hours I have had 3 winning trades,

(pound, nz and cad) based on the 4 hour. For me there are enough

"high quality" opportunities per day with this method that I will

ignore setups from the lower timeframe.

(not that there's anything wrong with that

--- 帖子 #1766 ---
If any of you use scripts to set your buy or sell and are MQL savvy you can put this in your script to save a screenshot at time of entry in the  experts/files dir

if (TakeScreenShot == true)

if(!WindowScreenShot(StringConcatenate(NAME + "-" + Symbol(),"-",Period(),"-",TimeToStr(TimeCurrent(),TIME_DATE),"-",Hour(),"H",Minute(),".gif"),size_x,size_y))

Print(GetLastError());

and declare your variables

extern bool   TakeScreenShot  = true;

extern int       size_x = 1280;

extern int       size_y = 720;

Please dont ask for my script as its not mine and I dont want to release it due to copyright

also set your scripts up as hotkeys ie ALT B buy ALT S sell

--- 帖子 #1777 ---
I use the simplest method available

i take a chart, i look at the lh side and see where the price was, i look at the rh side and see where the price is

if rh is clearly lower then downtrend, rh clearly higher then uptrend, otherwise rangebound

simple but effective

so for me (regardless what the stochs say) i see

gu down

eu down

au down

usdchf rangebound

ej down

usdcad rangebound

BUT this is my opinion only

--- 帖子 #1793 ---
there is quite a few

there is the 1-Retracement Finder by mediator - NOTE, this only checks the 60m stoch and has a bug in it where it checks for Stoch EMA on High/Low instead of Stoch LWMA on Close/Close

there is the !RF Double Stoch posted by me a few days ago, this only checks the stochs and RF

there is the !Retrace Finder posted by me yesterday (for this indi to work you need to have "TMA Called" in your MT4), this only alerts on the RF,Stochs AND TMA being in alignment

Paperclip can help you find them, instructions are there on the appropriate post as well.

--- 帖子 #1816 ---
I thought you were getting the idea, now you seem to have gone backwards

Why would you enter a long EURCHF

and don't say because the 4hr stoch turned upwards, just because the long term stoch terms upwards doesn't necessarily mean the trend has changed.

for instance, if the stoch goes up by 0.00001 greater than the previous it will be classed as upwards

Be EXTREMELY careful of stoch changes especially when in extreme OB/OS conditions

make sure the stoch has changed by some distance and for a number of bars

In your conversations with P.Porter you agreed the trend was down, nothing has changed since then.

The idea with the Up/Down indication is purely for help.  A computer does not care if it is 0.00001 greater than the previous or 50.00000 it classes both as UP.

--- 帖子 #1817 ---
yep huge mistake

but we or i even can take this as a positive learning curve. What i learnt is on the 5 min chart trend is clearly going down with lower highs etc so do not long even if all signals line up, am i in the ball park here?

--- 帖子 #1818 ---
This is applicable to ALL systems you try out, not just this one

just because the rules say to go long, look at what the PA is telling you

maybe in the trading systems thread we should ban the word "rules" and use "guidelines" instead

General -

Trying to catch the beginning of a trend change is extremely hard and you will be burnt 9 times out of 10

A trend once established will ALWAYS have at least one retracement where you can enter

For this method -

The thread is called retracement - if you don't have a retracement then you shouldn't be entering (and here I mean a PA retracement not the retracement finder indicator going red/blue/magenta.... whatever color)

The exception of course is with the short term band 2 band method when the market is ranging, because then it is just zig-zagging between the bands

--- 帖子 #1835 ---
The problem is that the indi's are 'custom' indi's. Custom indis invariably consist of calls to standard indi's.

TMA With Distance, for example, makes several calls to other indicators. This happens at each tick over several charts. The system uses three custom indi's, so the cpu takes a hammering.

Mostly this is not a problem, but becomes one if you have much more going on in the background.

The solution is a brand-spanking new computer with the latest mega-memory and cpu that will blow a hole in warp-space.

No, I haven't got one either. Hey ho. I restrict myself to the 5 charts recommended by Kevin, so my machine keeps on running.

--- 帖子 #1927 ---
It's VERY rare to find a straight up technical system that works great as a stand alone system, think about it for a minute - what if our system is giving us an alert to buy right in an area where "the big boys" are unloading their inventory, who's going to win that trade - your $20 or their $20M ?

If you do learn some price action (most importantly supply/demand) then you will be able to see where the pros have a lot of orders in (just waiting) to buy or sell at certain levels. Then you can position yourself in the right direction and scalp all day long with this awesome short-term market timing system.

That's my approach and it's going great, I'm really pleased with this method's ability to time and show exactly where the entrances and exits are.

To learn the supply and demand, I recommend to watch all of these webinars and study them, it will pay off big.

http://www.fxstreet.com/search/contr...1-e9bf77216d2f

cheers

--- 帖子 #1933 ---
Hi HappyHappy/All

just watched a few of the webinars, one that was VERY interesting when combined with this method is the one on CCI & Stochastics.

In the original rules of this method we enter on after the first bar in the Retrace Finder in the direction of our trade, ie. for long the first bar where the CCI was greater than 0, for short the first bar where the CCI was less than 0

In the webinar he mentions using CCI & Stochs (either one works) and using the "turn" (although it is easier to see on the stochs as you also have the signal line)

This combats the problem I have often found that by the time the CCI confirms the trade, the price is often past the mid-line which makes for a riskier trade.

However the important  point to note is, that it is very important which OB/OS signals to take (he uses +100/-100 for OB/OS on CCI)

so in this method for MOM trades if the 4hr stoch is up, then you only take OS signals, 4hr stoch down only take OB signals.

As I have non-repainting versions of all indicators I have visually looked and the signals generated are usually 1 to 2 candles earlier, which means

a) less problems with the mid-line

b) reduced risk on SL as you are entering sooner after the swing low/high

As it's quite late here, will be running thru a full forward test tomorrow for MOM trades only.

I will post a report on my findings (as the only true method of testing is forward testing)

Best Regards

John

--- 帖子 #1938 ---
FYI, the Retracement Finder indicator is nothing more that a CCI(8) converted to a Histogram indicator where it signals the turn from <= 0 to > 0 for a Long signal or the turn from >= 0 to < 0 for a Short signal.

Still a useful indicator if you don't want to hurt your eyes looking at the normal CCI(8) indicator

Hi J,

yes.. several mistakes..

One for most..  this pair is and was at the time of your entry in a super range mood (under 30 daily range).. you need enough room to even play ping pong.. lol

Two.. super narrow band.. not enough to get in and get out for good enough profit, if and when it does go in your direction considering the spread and the buffer (which is wise to use) to come out ahead at the end.
