--- 帖子 #1990 ---
Hi All

don't know if this helps anyone else, but for me I find it useful,

I ignore the direction/colors of the 4hr stoch once it is in OB/OS

I just assume that while it remains in OB it is bullish, OS it is bearish

Reason being is that we are looking at the 4hr stoch on a 5m timeframe, it can remain in OB/OS for a longgggg time, just because it has move slightly down / up, while it is on the OB/OS zone doesn't necessarily mean the trend has changed.

Of course once it is out of these zones then the color/direction matters.

Just my observation of course, for me it's helped.

Regards, John

--- 帖子 #1998 ---
Hi Johntan

it is not a must, but gives you less risk.

The TMA bands can be thought of as another oscillator

the upper band is Overbought, the lower band is Oversold

General rule of thumb for oscillators is you try to buy close to oversold, sell close to overbought

A lot of people use the mid-line of the TMA as the latest possible risk, although be aware in strongly trending markets the price may not retrace to even the mid-line.

Regards, John

--- 帖子 #2002 ---
Hi Globalinvest

the problem is the indicator you are basing your alert on.

the color stochastic indicator you attached, simply compares the current stochastic value with the previous, and paints all lines in that time period with the same value.

so in theory on an hourly stoch the following could happen

open of the hour, stoch is up

15m into the hour, stoch is down

30m into the hour, stoch is equal

45m into the hour stoch is up again

on the indicator you are using all you would see is the final value, which is up, but during the hour it went down then back up,

Regards, John

--- 帖子 #2010 ---
yeah, I think you missed the point I was trying to make

this indicator repaints the current bar (like all indicator) - but remember this is the current bar on the other timeframe

so my example again of 1hr MTF stoch, on a 5m chart

12 5m bars make up the hour

so when it repaints the current bar on the MTF timeframe, it can repaint upto 11 candles back on the 5m

only when the hour bar is closed, is the 12 5m candles that make up that bar not repainted anymore.

--- 帖子 #2029 ---
I am going to give you guys a tip in regards to MOM trade when it don't fit into perfect setup scenario and ends up missing out on profit opportunities..

I have displayed a chart from yesterdays A/U action..  as you all see it was in a slow bullish move all day.. which it did not give us the perfect mom setup while it was moving on with momentum behind it..

so the problem is.. at times it does not come in although way to make a opposite band touch before releasing with energy for possible profit..

so i recommend.. when you see such PA... disregard the band only if you got the 3 points below in line..

watch the chart..

disregard the perfect band touch.. if:

1) both 4hr and 1hr (30m) are in the same direction

2) CCI to be OS on buy  and OB on sell..(this could be the substitute of band for you in this case only)

3) when you got a minimum +10 pips gap between your entry point based of RF to HH/LL..

if these three criteria is meet.. go for it regardless of the Price touching the opposite band.. all you need is a good enough PB to get on such rides.

this past week I personally made a lot of positive pips on such plays..   the important point in the MOM trade is that the MOMENTUM is there.. if yes..than don't let the arrival of perfect setup to stand in your way of profitability.

I hope it helps you out.

Hey guys, just took an easy 30 pips on the eur/usd. what i have found is if you use heiken ashi instead of candles and wait until price goes over sold or over bought on the tma lines. buy or sell when the heiken ashi changes colour and candle closes as long as it still below or above tma lines. i set my target to the opposit far tma line. the heiken ashi seems to change colour either at the same time as the retracement finder or 1 bar before which gives you that slightly better entry. will keep testing and if anyone interested will let you know how it going.

--- 帖子 #2088 ---
no,

you have entered a buy when the 4hr stoch is clearly down

a mom trade is inline with the 4hr stoch from the opposite band

ie. 4hr stoch down, sell trade from upper band

4hr stoch up, buy trade from lower band

I would suggest you read the rules again.

regards, John

--- 帖子 #2135 ---
oh my mistake then.. my apology..

sure i give it out..

but I also said if i see enough interest as i don't want people to think I am forcing anything or show boating etc.. you know how one can get attacked for no reasons in forums in general.. you come with the best intention and get slammed all of sudden.. lol

but i must warn its nothing super technical.. it's just something simple i use.

ok to everyone..

its called the 4th minute of the 5 minute candle..

for example..

when the RF signal goes off or you get a candle that is breaking back inside the band that your looking to get in the action off the OB or OS or mom.. instead of getting in right away on the first 3minutes of the candle or the beginning stage of it.. or waiting for the full candle to close and getting in on the next candle..

instead of both those scenarios... wait up to the arrival of the 4th minute of the candle... IF it has shaped into solid candle in your direction than you can enter within that 4th minute... whatever the candle shape is up to the 4th minute it will most times stay the same or better and not change most times to completely a different look on the last minute of it..

so if i choose to make a early entry it will be in this fashion.

I hope it's find useful.. it's just a tip from a brother..

--- 帖子 #2141 ---
well John my friend.. what i have found is that people are full of comments, excitement and etc, when market is alive and kicking and other times not so much so.. when market is ranging and not alive most people lose money or not make as much so it's natural to either quit for the day or stay quiet, or worse go on tilt and not to come to talk about it.. lol

but on the same token, the fact of the matter is that a Trader becomes "A Trader" when he can bear with these days the same as the good days... if you all ask me for example, I have learned and find tuned things awful a lot more on bad range/chop days verses the good alive trending days.. one's true skill would get build stronger from handling the range and choppy days no matter what system you use at some point you will have to face it.. sometimes its easy to avoid the range days in total, but chop days are impossible bcz it keeps you on your toes and it makes you think that this is the one that can run or make profit on..

anyways, that's why i choose to stay more active even more on such days in forum bcz that's the time to help and get help and not to get bored mean time.. so its a win win situation.. and if everyone could do the same, i think only good could come out of it if trading is your goal and passion.

for example the first two weeks of this thread.. market was really hot.. there was runs and runners left and right overall it was alive market..  the last two weeks, not so glamorous..  but the questions is in which period we learned more and made the necessary adjustments up to now so we can successed on both period and more importantly to avoid vanishing our accounts..  i think everyone should know the answer..

i think John has been perfect example as to keep monitoring and coming up with different tools and etc, for better results.. but i don't think he would be as more active if he was making 50 100+ like the first week..

so John my hats off to you bud.

just some words from the guy next door everyone, don't take anything i say too serious.. lol

--- 帖子 #2146 ---
following up on john's post.. about one knowing his weakness/strength and exit..

my weakness is to take action on every valid opportunities.. not being present all the time..

but about exit... i just go with amusing the worse at first always.. IMHO its impossible to know , feel, assume or predict what kind of a market is in store for us starting our days out or even mid day or end of the day,, this damn thing can run or make sideways PA on a blink.. as soon as one decides to scalp for the day.. market will take one direction on one signal and runs to the moon and when decides go for runners, market will go sideways till you get sick to your stomach.. both can result in damages once market fuck with the mental..

so, when I enter a trade on top of the key (bands ob/os) my first intention/expectations out that trade is to exit at the other side of the band if its not presented with a clear strong break of the band.. so on other word i start as a scalp mentality and what i get beyond it would be a bonus .. even though i really gun for longer profit, a runner like.. it's only kept in back of my mind but with hawks eye on the band price action.. so I  would not hesitate to take the profit on wishy-washy action at the band.. I actually grade myself on such exits.. other day i made terrible decision on banking with G/U while it was a clear strong break of the band.. i got +17 PA ran for 120.. me as a trader that little part is a make or break for me.. and it's superbly vital in this system to not exit prematurely on clean strong break when its visible easily..

now, this works with this system.. for two reasons.. 1) bcz we get plenty of opportunities even on rangy sluggish days, so a +5 +10 here and there will sum up to a good amount at end of the day like docrock results..2) this system skins the cat in two ways... ranging market and trending market.. so could be always in the action to get your chunk.

with these two luxury at hand.. it's ok to bank less than your risk.. our true risk in most setups is 20 25pips.. but with high hit ratio when banking +10's.. you can make pretty good bottom line at the end of the week or month even on most days..

that's my take on the exit issue.

again this is just me.. do what makes sense to you.. what fits your plan and goals and simply what seems right for you overall.

--- 帖子 #2155 ---
Hi Vicky,

welcome to the thread..

you wait for one of the stoch's to turn in the reversal direction normally the 1hr (30m) first.. and then more importantly you'll wait for the band to lose its form of striking in one direction and turns into a more of a settle or flat or semi flat at least before you take your first shot at it.. this only if you got a trend in your hand meaning 80-100 plus move in one direction..

but also remember when your on a trend your mostly looking firstly for MOM trade.. meaning the first retrace at some point to reach the opposite band.. so this helps you to sit on your hands patiently to not get involve in the middle of the NO MAN's LAND.. you should know what that is: yes you guessed it.. the correction.

I hope it helps.

Hi,

keep it simple..

TP.. keep a eye on +10 on every trade.. than the reach of the band.. than the break or stall at the band.. than break of each level such as daily ranges..

I highly recommend to not let yourself in control of any indicator to tell you what to do.. especially on exit.

--- 帖子 #2230 ---
in a long trend

put a fibonnacci from the low to the high (so the zero line is at the high), then look for a retrace at least to the 38.2 line

in a short trend the reverse

if you look at the audusd open picture i uploaded you can see my fib.

fibs are used quite a lot in various retracement methods, i just also use it in this one

--- 帖子 #2241 ---
if you were using the TMA True (with distances), you would have seen that this was a risky trade to take

that is the problem with the originally recomended TMA indicator, hence most people use the true version now.

the difference between true and the repaint, is that you would have see that the TMA bands were definitely bearish, for a bullish trade they should be either bullish or neutral (flat or almost)

the picture below shows how it looked on mine - the bands were bearish, even the previous bullish move didn't manage to flatten them out

--- 帖子 #2254 ---
Hi

couple of points on your last trades:-

EURGBP - why would you place a buy? the tma bands were clearly against you

USDCHF - your trailing stop was too close, the entry was fine, the stop loss should have been about 0.81595, this has not been touched, by my rough calculations the price hasn't even gone up by more than 15 pips yet

AUDJPY - couple of points, your fib placement, for me the fib should go on the whole of the wave, the first retracement that occurred was not nearly big enough to consider the second move down as a new wave

However that said, with the price already well below the TMA bands, your first target should have been the zero line which it hit

there are 2 main price areas you need to concentrate on in this method when in a trade, how the price reacts at the various band levels, and if using the fib, how the price reacts at the zero line

unless it breaks through these areas with no problem you should be looking to exit

All this has been explained numerous times in the forum, I suggest you go back and read again, particularly helpful are the posts from P.Dean.

In regards to waves and fibs there are various resources and information available on this forum and the web

Regards, John

USDCHF - your trailing stop was too close, the entry was fine, the stop  loss should have been about 0.81595, this has not been touched, by my  rough calculations the price hasn't even gone up by more than 15 pips  yet

Thanks for your insight. I am tring different stops.

AUDJPY - couple of points, your fib placement, for me the fib should go  on the whole of the wave, the first retracement that occurred was not  nearly big enough to consider the second move down as a new wave

However that said, with the price already well below the TMA bands, your  first target should have been the zero line which it hit

It was a long time ago that I studied fib., but I was egar to try them with this method, maybe I was too eager this time.

there are 2 main price areas you need to concentrate on in this method  when in a trade, how the price reacts at the various band levels, and if  using the fib, how the price reacts at the zero line

unless it breaks through these areas with no problem you should be looking to exit

All this has been explained numerous times in the forum, I suggest you  go back and read again, particularly helpful are the posts from P.Dean.

In regards to waves and fibs there are various resources and information available on this forum and the web

I  read through the whole thread, but there are some controversal info,  and different apporoaches. I try out every apporoach and also mix them  for best results.

--- 帖子 #2256 ---
Hi Balasz227

regarding the first point that I made regarding the TMA bands being against you, this is my personal take

i will occasionally take these, if the price action gives me a reason, the fact that the CCI indicates short/long is not enough reason for me

one method that serves me well, is to look for a 123 pattern to return me to the trend direction after a long retrace (and generally this also "flattens" out the TMA bands a bit)

unfortunately the thread owner no longer participates in the thread, though I am sure that he has lots of filters he uses that he just didn't mention.

P.Dean and others have tried to fill in these "missing" gaps with their own insights, likewise myself.

In the end, what occurs is you take the basic methodology and apply your own style, in the end creating a system that YOU can work with (if you look at some of my later screenshots you will notice my screens do not have stochastics or cci)

What works for others may not work for you.

In the end 90% of the systems in this forum are basically the same, trend following - they may use different indicators but a lot of the entry signals are roughly the same, the reason being almost all indicators are based off candle prices (with the exception of volume indicators) therefore if one signals a buy/sell another one is likely to do so as well.

Regards, John

--- 帖子 #2260 ---
hi

mid-line is a linear weighted moving avg of x periods (default 56)

upper and lower lines are an average true range multiplier (default 2) of x periods (default 100)

--- 帖子 #2276 ---
nice job on banking and lowering the risk.

the only reason i allowed myself to make comments it's bcz i see in your trades you disregard one of the most important things.. and that is.. ignoring the band.. OB/OS issue which is the cornerstone of this method and in trading in general..

your goal is to get on sell when is most over bought on a neutral or favorable band and vise verse and set you eyes and heart firstly on banking at opposite band PA reaction.. if it don't break it strong.. bank the +10/+15.. but if you get in late or on the bottom of the band than the risk too high for a possible reward.

I hope it make sense.
